### **Strategies to Use NLP for Better Texting with Amanda**
#### **1. Make Statements That Imply a Response Instead of Asking Direct Questions**
Instead of:  
‚ùå *‚ÄúDid you get home okay?‚Äù* (which she ignored for a while)

‚úÖ **‚ÄúI was picturing you finally making it home, warming up, and settling in. Must‚Äôve felt good after a weekend like that.‚Äù**

---

#### **2. Use Assumptive Language to Lead the Conversation**
Instead of:
